        <h1 class="entry-title">

        <p id="h-simple-but-impressive-this-no-bake-cheesecake-is-a-real-crowd-pleaser-the-white-chocolate-and-boysenberry-flavours-make-it-an-absolute-treat">
         Simple but impressive, this no bake cheesecake is a real crowd pleaser. The white chocolate and boysenberry flavours make it an absolute treat!
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Disclaimer:
          <strong>
           This post is a paid partnership with Countdown Supermarkets. All content and opinions are my own.
          </strong>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <span id="more-12479">
        </span>
        <figure class="wp-block-image size-full">
         <img alt="Berry cheesecake on white marble background. One piece of cheesecake on a white plate with frozen boysenberries and a fork" class="wp-image-12492" data-skip-lazy="" decoding="async" fetchpriority="high" height="1125" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" src="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8.jpg" srcset="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8.jpg 750w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-720x1080.jpg 720w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-360x540.jpg 360w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-180x270.jpg 180w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-150x225.jpg 150w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-300x450.jpg 300w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-600x900.jpg 600w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-40x60.jpg 40w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-8-60x90.jpg 60w" width="750"/>
        </figure>
        <p>
         Hey cheesecake lovers...I have got a real treat for you today!
        </p>
        <p>
         Countdown NZ sent me a mystery box full of Own Brand ingredients and challenged me to come up with a recipe using only the ingredients in the box plus a few extra pantry staples.
        </p>
        <p>
         I put together the delicious ingredients that they sent me and created this show stopping boysenberry &amp; white chocolate no bake cheesecake, and it’s a winner!
        </p>
        <p>
         It has everything you love about traditional baked cheesecake but without the hassle of water baths and stressing over cracked tops. The filling is creamy, decadent and holds together perfectly once set.
        </p>
        <p>
         The base is made up of crushed gingernut biscuits which gives the cheesecake an awesome flavour and helps offset the sweetness of the white chocolate.
        </p>
        <figure class="wp-block-image size-full">
         <img alt="Gingernut biscuit cheesecake base in cake tin" class="wp-image-12486" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-lazy-src="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1.jpg 750w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1-150x225.jpg 150w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1-300x450.jpg 300w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-1-600x900.jpg 600w" decoding="async" height="1125" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20750%201125'%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="750"/>

        </figure>
        <figure class="wp-block-image size-full">

          <img alt="Cheesecake filling in glass bowl with spatula" class="wp-image-12487" decoding="async" height="1125" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" src="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2.jpg" srcset="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2.jpg 750w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2-150x225.jpg 150w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2-300x450.jpg 300w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-2-600x900.jpg 600w" width="750"/>
         </noscript>
        </figure>
        <p>
         The berry sauce swirled throughout the filling not only adds a beautiful pop of colour but adds a nice tang that complements the creamy filling perfectly.
        </p>
        <figure class="wp-block-image size-full">
         <img alt="Boysenberry filling for cheesecake in glass bowl" class="wp-image-12488" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-lazy-src="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3.jpg 750w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-150x225.jpg 150w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-300x450.jpg 300w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-600x900.jpg 600w" decoding="async" height="1125" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20750%201125'%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="750"/>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Boysenberry filling for cheesecake in glass bowl" class="wp-image-12488" decoding="async" height="1125" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" src="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3.jpg" srcset="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3.jpg 750w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-150x225.jpg 150w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-300x450.jpg 300w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-3-600x900.jpg 600w" width="750"/>
         </noscript>
        </figure>
        <p>
         Make this cheesecake up to 2 days ahead of time if you are planning on entertaining, which leaves you free to enjoy spending time with your guests on the day! It also freezes really well - wrap tightly and then thaw in the fridge for 24 hours before serving!
        </p>
        <figure class="wp-block-image size-full">
         <img alt="Boysensberry white chocolate cheesecake in springform cake tin" class="wp-image-12490" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-lazy-src="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6.jpg 750w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6-150x225.jpg 150w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6-300x450.jpg 300w, https://www.thekiwicountrygirl.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Boysenberry-White-Chocolate-Cheesecake-6-600x900.jpg 600w" decoding="async" height="1125" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20750%201125'%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="750"/>

             Boysenberry White Chocolate No Bake Cheesecake
            </h2>
            <div class="wprm-spacer" style="height: 5px">
            </div>
            <div class="wprm-recipe-summary wprm-block-text-normal">
             <span style="display: block;">
              Simple but impressive, this no bake cheesecake is a real crowd pleaser. The white chocolate and boysenberry flavours make it an absolute treat!
             </span>

                2 x 225
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">
                gram
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">
                blocks cream cheese
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">
                , softened
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" data-uid="7" style="list-style-type: none;">
               <span class="wprm-checkbox-container">
                <input aria-label=" 2 Tablespoons caster sugar" class="wprm-checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-6" type="checkbox"/>
                <label class="wprm-checkbox-label" for="wprm-checkbox-6">
                 <span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">
                  ▢
                 </span>
                </label>
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">
                2
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">
                Tablespoons
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">
                caster sugar
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" data-uid="8" style="list-style-type: none;">
               <span class="wprm-checkbox-container">
                <input aria-label=" 2 Tablespoons icing sugar (optional for a slightly sweeter and thicker cheesecake)" class="wprm-checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-7" type="checkbox"/>
                <label class="wprm-checkbox-label" for="wprm-checkbox-7">
                 <span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">
                  ▢
                 </span>
                </label>
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">
                2
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">
                Tablespoons
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">
                icing sugar
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">
                (optional for a slightly sweeter and thicker cheesecake)
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" data-uid="9" style="list-style-type: none;">
               <span class="wprm-checkbox-container">
                <input aria-label=" 1 teaspoon lemon juice" class="wprm-checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-8" type="checkbox"/>
                <label class="wprm-checkbox-label" for="wprm-checkbox-8">
                 <span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">
                  ▢
                 </span>
                </label>
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">
                1
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">
                teaspoon
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">
                lemon juice
               </span>
              </li>
             </ul>
            </div>
            <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
             <h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name wprm-block-text-bold">
              BERRY SWIRL
             </h4>
             <ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
              <li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" data-uid="11" style="list-style-type: none;">
               <span class="wprm-checkbox-container">
                <input aria-label=" 1 cup frozen boysenberries , thawed and drained" class="wprm-checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-9" type="checkbox"/>
                <label class="wprm-checkbox-label" for="wprm-checkbox-9">
                 <span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">
                  ▢
                 </span>
                </label>
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">
                1
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">
                cup
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">
                frozen boysenberries
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">
                , thawed and drained
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" data-uid="12" style="list-style-type: none;">
               <span class="wprm-checkbox-container">
                <input aria-label=" 1 Tablespoon maple syrup" class="wprm-checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-10" type="checkbox"/>
                <label class="wprm-checkbox-label" for="wprm-checkbox-10">
                 <span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">
                  ▢
                 </span>
                </label>
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">
                1
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">
                Tablespoon
               </span>
               <span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">
                maple syrup
               </span>
              </li>
             </ul>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-12480-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="12480">
            <h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">
             Instructions
            </h3>
            <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
             <ul class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-0" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                <span style="display: block;">
                 Put the frozen berries in a small sieve to thaw and drain over a bowl. Once thawed, press out most of the liquid and discard, and add the thawed berries to a small saucepan with the maple syrup. Cook over a medium heat for 5 minutes until the sauce thickens slightly. Remove from heat and put in the fridge to cool until needed.
                </span>
               </div>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-1" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                <span style="display: block;">
                 Crush the biscuits using a food processor, blender or in a bag with a rolling pin. Stir in the caster sugar and melted butter and press into a 23cm/9 inch round springform cake tin. Use a measuring cup to make sure the base is pressed down really firmly so that it holds together when set. Place the tin in the fridge to start setting.
                </span>
               </div>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-2" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                In a heatproof bowl combine ¼ cup of the cream with the chocolate and microwave in 20 second increments, stirring each time until melted or place the bowl over a pot of water on a medium heat and stir until melted. Allow to cool slightly.
               </div>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-3" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                Using a handheld or stand mixer with the whisk attachment, whip the remaining cream until stiff peaks form. Set aside.
               </div>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-4" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                Using a handheld or stand mixer with the paddle attachment whip the cream cheese and caster sugar for 3-4 minutes on medium-high speed until the mixture is fluffy and there are no lumps of cream cheese. Add the chocolate/cream mixture, icing sugar (if using) and lemon juice and mix on medium-high speed for a further 2-3 minutes, until the mixture lightens in colour and is fluffy. Gently fold through the whipped cream.
               </div>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-5" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                Spoon half of the filling onto the biscuit base. Drop 3-4 tablespoons of berry sauce on top of the filling and use a fork to swirl through the filling. Repeat with the remaining filling and berry sauce.
               </div>
              </li>
              <li class="wprm-recipe-instruction" id="wprm-recipe-12480-step-0-6" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
               <div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;">
                Refrigerate for at least 6 hours and up to 48 hours (overnight is preferable) before serving.
               </div>
              </li>
             </ul>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div id="recipe-video">
           </div>
           <div class="wprm-call-to-action wprm-call-to-action-simple" style="color: #ffffff;background-color: #385f2b;margin: 0px;padding-top: 10px;padding-bottom: 10px;">
            <span class="wprm-recipe-icon wprm-call-to-action-icon">
             <svg height="16" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
              <g class="nc-icon-wrapper" fill="#ffffff">
               <path d="M12,2.162c3.204,0,3.584,0.012,4.849,0.07c1.366,0.062,2.633,0.336,3.608,1.311 c0.975,0.975,1.249,2.242,1.311,3.608c0.058,1.265,0.07,1.645,0.07,4.849s-0.012,3.584-0.07,4.849 c-0.062,1.366-0.336,2.633-1.311,3.608c-0.975,0.975-2.242,1.249-3.608,1.311c-1.265,0.058-1.645,0.07-4.849,0.07 s-3.584-0.012-4.849-0.07c-1.366-0.062-2.633-0.336-3.608-1.311c-0.975-0.975-1.249-2.242-1.311-3.608 c-0.058-1.265-0.07-1.645-0.07-4.849s0.012-3.584,0.07-4.849c0.062-1.366,0.336-2.633,1.311-3.608 c0.975-0.975,2.242-1.249,3.608-1.311C8.416,2.174,8.796,2.162,12,2.162 M12,0C8.741,0,8.332,0.014,7.052,0.072 c-1.95,0.089-3.663,0.567-5.038,1.942C0.639,3.389,0.161,5.102,0.072,7.052C0.014,8.332,0,8.741,0,12 c0,3.259,0.014,3.668,0.072,4.948c0.089,1.95,0.567,3.663,1.942,5.038c1.375,1.375,3.088,1.853,5.038,1.942 C8.332,23.986,8.741,24,12,24s3.668-0.014,4.948-0.072c1.95-0.089,3.663-0.567,5.038-1.942c1.375-1.375,1.853-3.088,1.942-5.038 C23.986,15.668,24,15.259,24,12s-0.014-3.668-0.072-4.948c-0.089-1.95-0.567-3.663-1.942-5.038 c-1.375-1.375-3.088-1.853-5.038-1.942C15.668,0.014,15.259,0,12,0L12,0z" fill="#ffffff">
               </path>
               <path d="M12,5.838c-3.403,0-6.162,2.759-6.162,6.162S8.597,18.162,12,18.162s6.162-2.759,6.162-6.162 S15.403,5.838,12,5.838z M12,16c-2.209,0-4-1.791-4-4s1.791-4,4-4s4,1.791,4,4S14.209,16,12,16z" data-color="color-2">
               </path>
               <circle cx="18.406" cy="5.594" data-color="color-2" r="1.44">
